sounds a bit hairy actually"}, {"timstamp": "2015-09-02 18:11", "user": "Torne:", "body": "russruss: it's relatively easy if you understand dynamic linking on the platform(s) you are targeting, it's just annoying"}, {"timstamp": "2015-09-02 18:12", "user": "Torne:", "body": "e.g. on systems like linux that use ELF, -fvisibility=hidden as a gcc arg will make every symbol hidden by default and you can mark the symbols you intend to expose as having visibility default with a function attribute"}, {"timstamp": "2015-09-02 18:12", "user": "Torne:", "body": "google for symbol visibility etc and you should find out a bunch of stuff :)"}], "label": "other"}
